### [123] [Adaptive Query Routing: A Tier-Based Framework for Hybrid Retrieval Across Financial, Legal, and Medical Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14222)
*Afshan Hashmi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了三种检索架构（向量RAG、树推理和自适应混合检索）在金融、法律和医疗领域的表现，发现树推理总体得分最高，但没有单一范式在所有查询复杂度层级上占优，支持开发基于查询复杂度和文档结构动态选择策略的自适应检索系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究显示向量RAG与基于推理的检索系统各有优势，但缺乏系统性的跨领域比较。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过实现和评估三种检索架构，引入查询复杂度基准，为开发更智能的自适应检索系统提供实证基础。

Method: 1) 实现并评估三种检索架构：向量RAG、树推理和提出的自适应混合检索；2) 引入四层查询复杂度基准；3) 采用GPT-4驱动的LLM-as-judge评估方法；4) 在金融、法律和医疗领域进行实验；5) 使用FinanceBench（150个专家标注的SEC文件问题）进行验证。

Result: 树推理获得最高总体得分（0.900），但没有单一范式在所有层级占优：向量RAG在多文档合成（Tier 4）上表现最佳（0.900），混合AHR在交叉引用（0.850）和多章节查询（0.929）上表现最好。交叉引用召回率：树基和混合方法达到100%，向量搜索为91.7%。FinanceBench验证：树推理0.938，混合AHR 0.901，向量RAG 0.821，树-向量质量差距扩大到11.7个百分点。

Conclusion: 不同检索范式在不同查询类型和文档结构下各有优势，支持开发能够根据查询复杂度和文档结构动态选择策略的自适应检索系统。树推理在复杂金融文档QA中表现突出，但混合方法在特定查询类型上更具优势。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become the standard paradigm for grounding Large Language Model outputs in external knowledge. Lumer et al. [1] presented the first systematic evaluation comparing vector-based agentic RAG against hierarchical node-based reasoning systems for financial document QA across 1,200 SEC filings, finding vector-based systems achieved a 68% win rate. Concurrently, the PageIndex framework [2] demonstrated 98.7% accuracy on FinanceBench through purely reasoning-based retrieval. This paper extends their work by: (i) implementing and evaluating three retrieval architectures: Vector RAG, Tree Reasoning, and the proposed Adaptive Hybrid Retrieval (AHR) across financial, legal, and medical domains; (ii) introducing a four-tier query complexity benchmark; and (iii) employing GPT-4-powered LLM-as-judge evaluation. Experiments reveal that Tree Reasoning achieves the highest overall score (0.900), but no single paradigm dominates across all tiers: Vector RAG wins on multi-document synthesis (Tier 4, score 0.900), while the Hybrid AHR achieves the best performance on cross-reference (0.850) and multi-section queries (0.929). Cross-reference recall reaches 100% for tree-based and hybrid approaches versus 91.7% for vector search, quantifying a critical capability gap. Validation on FinanceBench (150 expert-annotated questions on real SEC 10-K and 10-Q filings) confirms and strengthens these findings: Tree Reasoning scores 0.938, Hybrid AHR 0.901, and Vector RAG 0.821, with the Tree--Vector quality gap widening to 11.7 percentage points on real-world documents. These findings support the development of adaptive retrieval systems that dynamically select strategies based on query complexity and document structure. All code and data are publicly available.

User studies and semantic alignment analyses demonstrate that TRACE effectively supports sustainable decision-making while preserving recommendation quality and interactive responsiveness. TRACE is implemented on Google's Agent Development Kit, with full code, Docker setup, prompts, and a publicly available demo video to ensure reproducibility.

### [125] [FRESCO: Benchmarking and Optimizing Re-rankers for Evolving Semantic Conflict in Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14227)
*Sohyun An,Hayeon Lee,Shuibenyang Yuan,Chun-cheng Jason Chen,Cho-Jui Hsieh,Vijai Mohan,Alexander Min*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: FRESCO基准测试评估检索增强生成中的重排序器在动态信息环境下的表现，发现现有重排序器倾向于选择语义丰富但事实过时的文档，通过指令优化可提升27%性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重排序器基准主要在静态环境下评估，未能充分测试在信息演化场景下的性能，而现实系统经常需要在时间上不同的证据之间进行选择

Method: 引入FRESCO基准，通过将时效性查询与历史维基百科修订配对，测试重排序器能否优先选择事实最新的证据同时保持语义相关性；并研究指令优化框架来缓解问题

Result: 评估显示现有重排序器存在一致的失败模式：强烈偏向于较旧、语义丰富的文档，即使这些文档事实已过时；通过识别平衡演化与非演化知识任务的帕累托最优指令，在演化知识任务上获得高达27%的提升

Conclusion: FRESCO基准填补了重排序器在动态信息环境下评估的空白，揭示了现有方法的局限性，并展示了通过指令优化可以显著改善重排序器在时效性信息处理上的表现

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is a key approach to mitigating the temporal staleness of large language models (LLMs) by grounding responses in up-to-date evidence. Within the RAG pipeline, re-rankers play a pivotal role in selecting the most useful documents from retrieved candidates. However, existing benchmarks predominantly evaluate re-rankers in static settings and do not adequately assess performance under evolving information -- a critical gap, as real-world systems often must choose among temporally different pieces of evidence. To address this limitation, we introduce FRESCO (Factual Recency and Evolving Semantic COnflict), a benchmark for evaluating re-rankers in temporally dynamic contexts. By pairing recency-seeking queries with historical Wikipedia revisions, FRESCO tests whether re-rankers can prioritize factually recent evidence while maintaining semantic relevance. Our evaluation reveals a consistent failure mode across existing re-rankers: a strong bias toward older, semantically rich documents, even when they are factually obsolete. We further investigate an instruction optimization framework to mitigate this issue. By identifying Pareto-optimal instructions that balance Evolving and Non-Evolving Knowledge tasks, we obtain gains of up to 27% on Evolving Knowledge tasks while maintaining competitive performance on Non-Evolving Knowledge tasks.

### [126] [Controlling Authority Retrieval: A Missing Retrieval Objective for Authority-Governed Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14488)
*Andre Bacellar*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 论文提出控制权威检索（CAR）问题，解决在正式权威领域（法律、药品监管、软件安全）中检索有效前沿文档的挑战，区别于传统语义相似度检索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在权威知识积累的领域，后续文档可以正式废止先前文档，但语义上可能相距甚远。传统基于语义相似度的检索方法无法正确处理这种权威控制关系，导致检索结果包含已废止的无效文档。

Method: 1. 形式化控制权威检索（CAR）问题；2. 提出定理4（CAR正确性特征）给出检索集正确性的充要条件；3. 提出命题2（范围可识别性上界）建立最坏情况性能上限；4. 在三个真实世界语料库验证；5. 开发两阶段检索方法。

Result: 在三个真实语料库上验证：安全公告（密集检索TCA@5=0.270，两阶段0.975）、最高法院推翻案例（密集0.172，两阶段0.926）、FDA药品记录（密集0.064，两阶段0.774）。GPT-4o-mini实验显示密集RAG在39%查询中错误声称"未修补"，两阶段降至16%。

Conclusion: 控制权威检索是一个与语义相似度检索不同的数学问题，需要专门的方法。两阶段检索方法显著优于密集检索，在权威文档检索中能有效避免返回已废止文档。研究提供了基准数据集、领域适配器和评估工具。

Abstract: In any domain where knowledge accumulates under formal authority -- law, drug regulation, software security -- a later document can formally void an earlier one while remaining semantically distant from it. We formalize this as Controlling Authority Retrieval (CAR): recovering the active frontier front(cl(A_k(q))) of the authority closure of the semantic anchor set -- a different mathematical problem from argmax_d s(q,d). The two central results are: Theorem 4 (CAR-Correctness Characterization) gives necessary-and-sufficient conditions on any retrieved set R for TCA(R,q)=1 -- frontier inclusion and no-ignored-superseder -- independent of how R was produced. Proposition 2 (Scope Identifiability Upper Bound) establishes phi(q) as a hard worst-case ceiling: for any scope-indexed algorithm, TCA@k <= phi(q) * R_anchor(q), proved by an adversarial permutation argument. Three independent real-world corpora validate the proved structure: security advisories (Dense TCA@5=0.270, two-stage 0.975), SCOTUS overruling pairs (Dense=0.172, two-stage 0.926), FDA drug records (Dense=0.064, two-stage 0.774). A GPT-4o-mini experiment shows the downstream cost: Dense RAG produces explicit "not patched" claims for 39% of queries where a patch exists; Two-Stage cuts this to 16%. Four benchmark datasets, domain adapters, and a single-command scorer are released at https://github.com/andremir/car-retrieval.

</details>

### [128] [CPGRec+: A Balance-oriented Framework for Personalized Video Game Recommendations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14586)
*Xiping Li,Aier Yang,Jianghong Ma,Kangzhe Liu,Shanshan Feng,Haijun Zhang,Yi Zhao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: CPGRec+通过引入偏好感知的边重加权模块和LLM驱动的偏好表示生成模块，解决了游戏推荐中准确性与多样性的平衡问题，同时缓解了GNN模型的过平滑问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于GNN的游戏推荐系统主要关注准确性而忽视多样性，且未能充分考虑玩家-游戏交互中的重要性差异，这些差异反映了玩家的个人偏好，并可能加剧GNN模型的过平滑问题。同时，现有方法未能充分利用大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力和丰富知识来解决这些限制。

Method: 提出两个新模块：1) 偏好感知边重加权（PER）模块，为边分配带符号的权重，定性区分重要的玩家兴趣和厌恶，然后定量测量偏好强度以缓解图卷积中的过平滑问题；2) 偏好感知表示生成（PRG）模块，利用LLMs通过比较全局和个人兴趣来推理个人偏好，生成游戏和玩家的上下文描述，从而优化玩家和游戏的表示。

Result: 在两个Steam数据集上的实验表明，CPGRec+在准确性和多样性方面均优于最先进的模型。

Conclusion: CPGRec+通过结合偏好感知的边重加权和LLM驱动的表示生成，有效解决了游戏推荐中准确性与多样性的平衡问题，同时缓解了GNN的过平滑问题，为动态游戏环境提供了更先进的推荐系统。

Abstract: The rapid expansion of gaming industry requires advanced recommender systems tailored to its dynamic landscape. Existing Graph Neural Network (GNN)-based methods primarily prioritize accuracy over diversity, overlooking their inherent trade-off. To address this, we previously proposed CPGRec, a balance-oriented gaming recommender system. However, CPGRec fails to account for critical disparities in player-game interactions, which carry varying significance in reflecting players' personal preferences and may exacerbate over-smoothness issues inherent in GNN-based models. Moreover, existing approaches underutilize the reasoning capabilities and extensive knowledge of large language models (LLMs) in addressing these limitations. To bridge this gap, we propose two new modules. First, Preference-informed Edge Reweighting (PER) module assigns signed edge weights to qualitatively distinguish significant player interests and disinterests while then quantitatively measuring preference strength to mitigate over-smoothing in graph convolutions. Second, Preference-informed Representation Generation (PRG) module leverages LLMs to generate contextualized descriptions of games and players by reasoning personal preferences from comparing global and personal interests, thereby refining representations of players and games. Experiments on \textcolor{black}{two Steam datasets} demonstrate CPGRec+'s superior accuracy and diversity over state-of-the-art models. The code is accessible at https://github.com/HsipingLi/CPGRec-Plus.

</details>


### [129] [Category-based and Popularity-guided Video Game Recommendation: A Balance-oriented Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14598)
*Xiping Li,Jianghong Ma,Kangzhe Liu,Shanshan Feng,Haijun Zhang,Yutong Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: CPGRec是一个新的视频游戏推荐框架，通过三个模块平衡推荐准确性和多样性，解决了现有方法偏重准确性而忽视多样性的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视频游戏推荐系统过于注重准确性而忽视多样性，导致推荐结果单一；现有方法缺乏游戏间的严格连接来提升准确性；许多关注多样性的方法在邻居建模和消息传播时未能充分利用游戏类别和流行度等关键信息。

Method: 提出CPGRec框架，包含三个模块：1)准确性驱动模块，通过更严格的游戏连接增强推荐准确性；2)多样性驱动模块，在游戏图中连接不同类别的邻居，利用流行游戏节点放大长尾游戏的影响力；3)综合模块，结合前两个模块，使用新的负样本评分重加权方法来平衡准确性和多样性。

Result: 在Steam数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法能有效改进游戏推荐效果。

Conclusion: CPGRec框架通过平衡准确性和多样性，解决了现有视频游戏推荐系统的局限性，为游戏推荐提供了更全面的解决方案。

Abstract: In recent years, the video game industry has experienced substantial growth, presenting players with a vast array of game choices. This surge in options has spurred the need for a specialized recommender system tailored for video games. However, current video game recommendation approaches tend to prioritize accuracy over diversity, potentially leading to unvaried game suggestions. In addition, the existing game recommendation methods commonly lack the ability to establish strict connections between games to enhance accuracy. Furthermore, many existing diversity-focused methods fail to leverage crucial item information, such as item category and popularity during neighbor modeling and message propagation. To address these challenges, we introduce a novel framework, called CPGRec, comprising three modules, namely accuracy-driven, diversity-driven, and comprehensive modules. The first module extends the state-of-the-art accuracy-focused game recommendation method by connecting games in a more stringent manner to enhance recommendation accuracy. The second module connects neighbors with diverse categories within the proposed game graph and harnesses the advantages of popular game nodes to amplify the influence of long-tail games within the player-game bipartite graph, thereby enriching recommendation diversity. The third module combines the above two modules and employs a new negative-sample rating score reweighting method to balance accuracy and diversity. Experimental results on the Steam dataset demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed method in improving game recommendations. The dataset and source codes are anonymously released at: https://github.com/CPGRec2024/CPGRec.git.

</details>


### [130] [Uncertainty-aware Generative Learning Path Recommendation with Cognition-Adaptive Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14613)
*Xiangrui Xiong,Hang Liang,Baiyang Chen,Zifei Pan,Yanli Lee*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: U-GLAD是一个不确定性感知的生成式学习路径推荐框架，通过高斯LSTM建模认知状态不确定性，使用目标导向概念编码器个性化对齐学习目标，并采用扩散模型生成最优概念推荐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学习路径推荐方法存在两个主要问题：1）未能考虑历史交互中的不确定性（如侥幸猜对或意外失误）；2）缺乏对多样化学习目标的适应性。这些局限性影响了推荐的准确性和个性化程度。

Method: U-GLAD框架包含三个核心组件：1）高斯LSTM将认知状态建模为概率分布，捕捉学习者真实状态；2）目标导向概念编码器使用多头注意力和目标特定变换，动态对齐概念语义与个体学习目标；3）生成式扩散模型预测下一个最优概念的潜在表示，而非传统的判别式排序方法。

Result: 在三个公开数据集上的广泛评估表明，U-GLAD显著优于代表性基线方法。进一步分析证实了其在感知交互不确定性和提供稳定、目标驱动的推荐路径方面的卓越能力。

Conclusion: U-GLAD通过建模认知状态不确定性、目标导向概念编码和生成式扩散方法，有效解决了传统学习路径推荐中的局限性，实现了更准确、个性化且稳定的推荐效果。

Abstract: Learning Path Recommendation (LPR) is critical for personalized education, yet current methods often fail to account for historical interaction uncertainty (e.g., lucky guesses or accidental slips) and lack adaptability to diverse learning goals. We propose U-GLAD (Uncertainty-aware Generative Learning Path Recommendation with Cognition-Adaptive Diffusion). To address representation bias, the framework models cognitive states as probability distributions, capturing the learner's underlying true state via a Gaussian LSTM. To ensure highly personalized recommendation, a goal-oriented concept encoder utilizes multi-head attention and objective-specific transformations to dynamically align concept semantics with individual learning goals, generating uniquely tailored embeddings. Unlike traditional discriminative ranking approaches, our model employs a generative diffusion model to predict the latent representation of the next optimal concept. Extensive evaluations on three public datasets demonstrate that U-GLAD significantly outperforms representative baselines. Further analyses confirm its superior capability in perceiving interaction uncertainty and providing stable, goal-driven recommendation paths.

</details>


### [131] [Federated User Behavior Modeling for Privacy-Preserving LLM Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14833)
*Lei Guo,Hongyun Yang,Pengjie Ren,Tong Chen,Hui Liu,Zhumin Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: SF-UBM：一种语义增强的联邦用户行为建模方法，用于解决非重叠隐私保护跨域推荐问题，通过自然语言作为通用桥梁连接不同领域，结合知识蒸馏和对齐行为与语义空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推荐系统面临用户数据稀疏问题，跨域推荐方法通常假设领域重叠且可访问，但缺乏对隐私保护跨域推荐（PPCDR）的关注，特别是在非重叠领域设置下存在三大挑战：跨域对齐困难、数据模态异构、协同过滤信号与LLM特征空间不匹配。

Method: 提出SF-UBM方法：1）使用自然语言作为通用桥梁，通过语义增强的联邦架构连接不相交领域，加密共享基于文本的物品表示，用户数据保留本地；2）设计事实-反事实知识蒸馏模块，整合领域无关和领域特定知识；3）将预学习的用户偏好和跨域物品表示投影到软提示空间，对齐行为与语义空间。

Result: 在三个真实世界领域对上进行了广泛实验，结果显示SF-UBM相比最近的SOTA方法具有显著效果优势。

Conclusion: SF-UBM成功解决了非重叠隐私保护跨域推荐中的三大挑战，通过语义增强的联邦架构、知识蒸馏和空间对齐技术，实现了有效的跨域知识迁移和隐私保护推荐。

Abstract: Large Language Models have shown great success in recommender systems. However, the limited and sparse nature of user data often restricts the LLM's ability to effectively model behavior patterns. To address this, existing studies have explored cross-domain solutions by conducting Cross-Domain Recommendation tasks. But previous methods typically assume domains are overlapped and can be accessed readily. None of the LLM methods address the privacy-preserving issues in the CDR settings, that is, Privacy-Preserving Cross-Domain Recommendation. Conducting non-overlapping PPCDR with LLM is challenging since: 1)The inability to share user identity or behavioral data across domains impedes effective cross-domain alignment. 2)The heterogeneity of data modalities across domains complicates knowledge integration. 3)Fusing collaborative filtering signals from traditional recommendation models with LLMs is difficult, as they operate within distinct feature spaces. To address the above issues, we propose SF-UBM, a Semantic-enhanced Federated User Behavior Modeling method. Specifically, to deal with Challenge 1, we leverage natural language as a universal bridge to connect disjoint domains via a semantic-enhanced federated architecture. Here, text-based item representations are encrypted and shared, while user-specific data remains local. To handle Challenge 2, we design a Fact-counter Knowledge Distillation module to integrate domain-agnostic knowledge with domain-specific knowledge, across different data modalities. To tackle Challenge 3, we project pre-learned user preferences and cross-domain item representations into the soft prompt space, aligning behavioral and semantic spaces for effective LLM learning. We conduct extensive experiments on three pairs of real-world domains, and the experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of SF-UBM compared to the recent SOTA methods.

</details>


### [132] [Well Begun is Half Done: Training-Free and Model-Agnostic Semantically Guaranteed User Representation Initialization for Multimodal Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14839)
*Jinfeng Xu,Zheyu Chen,Shuo Yang,Jinze Li,Hewei Wang,Jianheng Tang,Wei Wang,Xiping Hu,Edith C. H. Ngai*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出SG-URInit方法，通过融合用户交互物品的模态特征和对应簇的全局特征，为多模态推荐中的用户表示提供语义丰富的初始化，弥补用户与物品表示之间的语义鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态推荐方法忽视了用户表示初始化的重要性。物品有丰富的模态信息可用于初始化，而用户表示通常随机初始化，导致用户与物品表示之间存在显著的语义鸿沟。

Method: 提出SG-URInit方法，为每个用户构建初始表示时，融合两个部分：1）用户交互过的物品的模态特征（局部语义）；2）这些物品对应簇的全局特征（全局语义）。该方法无需训练且与模型无关。

Result: 在多个真实数据集上的实验表明，将SG-URInit集成到先进的多模态推荐模型中能显著提升推荐性能。此外，该方法还能进一步缓解物品冷启动问题，并加速模型收敛。

Conclusion: SG-URInit是一种高效实用的多模态推荐解决方案，通过语义保证的用户表示初始化，有效弥补了用户与物品表示之间的语义鸿沟，提升推荐性能的同时不增加训练计算开销。

Abstract: Recent advancements in multimodal recommendations, which leverage diverse modality information to mitigate data sparsity and improve recommendation accuracy, have gained significant attention. However, existing multimodal recommendations overlook the critical role of user representation initialization. Unlike items, which are naturally associated with rich modality information, users lack such inherent information. Consequently, item representations initialized based on meaningful modality information and user representations initialized randomly exhibit a significant semantic gap.
  To this end, we propose a Semantically Guaranteed User Representation Initialization (SG-URInit). SG-URInit constructs the initial representation for each user by integrating both the modality features of the items they have interacted with and the global features of their corresponding clusters. SG-URInit enables the initialization of semantically enriched user representations that effectively capture both local (item-level) and global (cluster-level) semantics.
  Our SG-URInit is training-free and model-agnostic, meaning it can be seamlessly integrated into existing multimodal recommendation models without incurring any additional computational overhead during training. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world datasets demonstrate that incorporating SG-URInit into advanced multimodal recommendation models significantly enhances recommendation performance. Furthermore, the results show that SG-URInit can further alleviate the item cold-start problem and also accelerate model convergence, making it an efficient and practical solution for multimodal recommendations.

</details>


### [133] [GenRec: A Preference-Oriented Generative Framework for Large-Scale Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14878)
*Yanyan Zou,Junbo Qi,Lunsong Huang,Yu Li,Kewei Xu,Jiabao Gao,Binglei Zhao,Xuanhua Yang,Sulong Xu,Shengjie Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: GenRec是一个面向偏好的生成式推荐框架，通过页面级NTP训练、语义ID压缩和强化学习对齐，解决了生成式检索在工业部署中的三大挑战，在京东App上实现了显著的线上效果提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式检索通过下一个令牌预测为推荐提供了有前景的范式，但在扩展到大规模工业系统时面临三个主要挑战：1) 分页请求机制导致相同模型输入产生不一致输出；2) 基于语义ID的多令牌项目表示编码长用户行为序列成本过高；3) 生成策略与细微用户偏好信号的对齐困难。

Method: 提出了GenRec框架，包含三个核心技术：1) 页面级NTP任务，监督整个交互页面而非单个项目，提供更密集的梯度信号并解决点式训练的一对多歧义；2) 非对称线性令牌合并器，压缩提示中的多令牌语义ID，减少约2倍输入长度；3) GRPO-SR强化学习方法，结合组相对策略优化与NLL正则化保证稳定性，并使用混合奖励（密集奖励模型+相关性门控）缓解奖励黑客问题。

Result: 在为期一个月的在线A/B测试中，GenRec相比现有流水线实现了点击量提升9.5%，交易量提升8.7%的显著改进。

Conclusion: GenRec成功解决了生成式检索在工业部署中的关键挑战，通过统一的仅解码器架构实现了偏好对齐的高效推荐，证明了生成式检索在大规模生产环境中的可行性和优越性。

Abstract: Generative Retrieval (GR) offers a promising paradigm for recommendation through next-token prediction (NTP). However, scaling it to large-scale industrial systems introduces three challenges: (i) within a single request, the identical model inputs may produce inconsistent outputs due to the pagination request mechanism; (ii) the prohibitive cost of encoding long user behavior sequences with multi-token item representations based on semantic IDs, and (iii) aligning the generative policy with nuanced user preference signals. We present GenRec, a preference-oriented generative framework deployed on the JD App that addresses above challenges within a single decoder-only architecture. For training objective, we propose Page-wise NTP task, which supervises over an entire interaction page rather than each interacted item individually, providing denser gradient signal and resolving the one-to-many ambiguity of point-wise training. On the prefilling side, an asymmetric linear Token Merger compresses multi-token Semantic IDs in the prompt while preserving full-resolution decoding, reducing input length by ~2X with negligible accuracy loss. To further align outputs with user satisfaction, we introduce GRPO-SR, a reinforcement learning method that pairs Group Relative Policy Optimization with NLL regularization for training stability, and employs Hybrid Rewards combining a dense reward model with a relevance gate to mitigate reward hacking. In month-long online A/B tests serving production traffic, GenRec achieves 9.5% improvement in click count and 8.7% in transaction count over the existing pipeline.

</details>


### [134] [Metric-agnostic Learning-to-Rank via Boosting and Rank Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15101)
*Camilo Gomez,Pengyang Wang,Yanjie Fu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出一种新的列表式学习排序框架，通过可微排序损失函数和梯度提升机，解决传统LTR方法对单一排序指标的依赖问题，实现更高效和泛化性更强的排序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学习排序方法依赖单一前缀排序指标（如NDCG或MAP），存在两个主要问题：1）非可微问题：直接在排序指标上优化排序函数本质上是非平滑的，导致训练过程不稳定和低效；2）有限的排序效用：基于单一指标优化难以泛化到其他感兴趣的排序指标。

Method: 提出一种新颖的列表式LTR框架：1）设计新的可微排序损失函数，结合排序算子的平滑近似和每个查询的平均均方损失；2）采用梯度提升机来最小化针对每个列表提出的损失函数。

Result: 大量实验结果表明，该方法在信息检索指标上优于当前最先进方法，同时保持了相似的效率。

Conclusion: 提出的框架通过可微排序损失和梯度提升机，有效解决了传统LTR方法的局限性，实现了更高效和泛化性更强的排序性能。

Abstract: Learning-to-Rank (LTR) is a supervised machine learning approach that constructs models specifically designed to order a set of items or documents based on their relevance or importance to a given query or context. Despite significant success in real-world information retrieval systems, current LTR methods rely on one prefix ranking metric (e.g., such as Normalized Discounted Cumulative Gain (NDCG) or Mean Average Precision (MAP)) for optimizing the ranking objective function. Such metric-dependent setting limits LTR methods from two perspectives: (1) non-differentiable problem: directly optimizing ranking functions over a given ranking metric is inherently non-smooth, making the training process unstable and inefficient; (2) limited ranking utility: optimizing over one single metric makes it difficult to generalize well to other ranking metrics of interest. To address the above issues, we propose a novel listwise LTR framework for efficient and generalizable ranking purpose. Specifically, we propose a new differentiable ranking loss that combines a smooth approximation to the ranking operator with the average mean square loss per query. Then, we adapt gradient-boosting machines to minimize our proposed loss with respect to each list, a novel contribution. Finally, extensive experimental results confirm that our method outperforms the current state-of-the-art in information retrieval measures with similar efficiency.

</details>
